<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_692c8597-2bed-4671-a57a-efb9ce4fb737'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText16775463420788151933" style="display:none"><i>Librarian's note: An alternate cover edition can be found <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35005990.here" title="here" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a></i><br /><br />Danika hasn’t had an easy life. Being insanely attracted to bad boys has never helped make it easier. <br /><br />One look at Tristan, and every brain cell she possessed went up in smoke. This man was trouble with a capital T. It was a given.<br />She knew better. Bad boys were bad. Especially for her. Considering her history, it was crazy to think otherwise. So why did crazy have to feel so damn fine?<br /><br />For as long as she could remember, Danika had been focused on the future with single-minded purpose. Tristan came along and taught her everything there was to know about letting go, and living in the present. She fell, hard and deep. Of course, that only made her impact with the ground that much more devastating.<br /><br />Bad Things is about Tristan and Danika, and their train wreck of a love story. This series can be read as a standalone, or with the Up in the Air series.<br /><br />Bad Things is a full length novel, at roughly 105,000 words.<br />This book is intended for ages 18 and up.</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/994799-so-did-i-miss-anything-big-by-not">So... did I miss anything big by not reading the Up in the Air series first? I&#39;ve been trying to avoid trilogies but I&#39;m totally sucked in now.</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_994799'><a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F17377032-bad-things">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/994799-so-did-i-miss-anything-big-by-not">3 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/994799-so-did-i-miss-anything-big-by-not">Add your answer</a>
</li>
</ul>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/39224857-cevrine"><img alt="" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_100x100-6433b08cbe793211f55e184d39e84c4d.png" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/39224857-cevrine">Cevrine</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Honestly I think you would be fine. In the Up in the Air series you only see them in the future with obvious damaging baggage. They're not a couple, h<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Honestly I think you would be fine. In the Up in the Air series you only see them in the future with obvious damaging baggage. They're not a couple, however as a reader you question their relationship. And thats when Tristen and Danika's series answer all you questions.<br /><br />Moreover, I do suggest you read the Up in the Air series. Its one of the best I've read. James and Bianca's relationship is so much less complicated than Tristen and Danika which is really nice. I think it would actually be nice to read Bad Things first as it looks at the past and you get a feel on how James, Tristen and Frankie become friends. If you dont know what I'm talking about then this gives you a reason to read the book. definitly worth spending the time and energy on. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

It.” </blockquote></i></b>  <br>*fans self*<br><br>I loved this book!! It made me swoon, squee, and swear which pretty much is the perfect mix, right?<br><br>I couldn’t put it down. Another winner from R.K. Lilley!<br><br>When Tristan unexpectedly becomes a fixed part of Danika’s world, he throws her whole life out of whack. Fun, flirty, and bossy with a devilish charming that could get just about anyone to do just about anything, he was Trouble with a capital T and just what Danika was trying to avoid. He was ripped, tattooed and baked the hell of chocolate chip cookies. Oh, and did I mention the dimples yet? ‘cuz, SWOON!! I had to ask. “So what do you do?”<br><br>“Hookups. Brief, casual hookups. How about you?”<br><br>I shook my head, pursing my lips at him… “I do relationships. No exceptions. Never had a casual hookup in my life.”<br><br>He sighed… “Well I guess that makes things less complicated. Off the charts, scorching chemisty! Their banter had me smiling almost non-stop. Danika was sassy and sarcastic and Tristan was bossy and charmingly charismatic and their combination made for some absolutely brilliant scenes!<br><br><i> <blockquote> “You making a move on me?” I called out to him, but I wasn’t pushing him away…<br><br>His smile was innocent enough, but i thought there was a hint of something else in his eyes.<br><br>“Just dancing, sweetheart.” </blockquote></i> <br><br>The whole book just flowed. From start to finish it kept my attention and made me steadily fall deeper and deeper in love with the story and the characters.<br><br>They were opposites in so many ways. Danika only did relationships and Tristan only did hook ups. On the surface that might just seem like personality traits but in reality it was the heart breaking events from their past that had shaped them into people who needed that. Danika came from an abusive home and craved the commitment and stability of a loving relationship. Tristan had fallen in love young and had thrown himself wholeheartedly into a relationship only to have his heart broken and trodden on by the one person he was committed to. They both had trust issues and deep hurts but at the end of the day they both cared deeply for each other… it was just a question of admitting it to themselves.<br><br><b> <i> <blockquote> “Tell me not to kiss you.”<br><br>“Don’t kiss me.”<br><br>“Mean it.”<br><br>“I can’t.” </blockquote></i></b>  <br>I have to admit, I didn’t expect how strongly and completely I was going to fall for Tristan. But guys, I fell HARD. Oh my Lord! This guy baked, had tats and dimples. That alone would melt my heart but he was also the lead singer in a rock band, was insanely protective of Danika and took “charming” to a whole new level. The things he said just made me SWOOOOON. He cared SO much her. You could feel it in every action he made.<br><br>There were times when I wanted to shake him but my heart also broke for him. You could just tell that he was one of THE good guys. You know? The one’s who’ll put their everything on the line for their girl. But after having his heart broken before, he had become guarded – determined never to put himself in that position again. Ever. But something about Danika was different and brought out the part of him that wanted to commit… he just couldn’t. Not at first. It was so hard for him to give his heart over again. But what that meant was that when he did, it was that much more meaningful because it showed not only the depth of his feelings but also the depth of his trust.<br><br>And seriously, have I mentioned how protective he was? There is just something about an Alpha who is willing to do ANYTHING for his girl that just makes my heart race.<br><br>Danika was a strong-willed yet very sweet heroine. I took a strong liking to her and felt very sympathetic to the things she went through. It was nice to have a heroine I didn’t get frustrated with. Her back story was just plain horrible. Seriously, the poor girl!! Life had really screwed her over but I absolutely adored that Tristan not only wanted to hear about it but also wanted to talk with her about it, openly, honestly.<br><br>They built a wonderful friendship filled to the very brim with scorching sexual tension… no joke, we’re talking off the charts hotness here! No kink, but Tristan was definitely Dominant in the bedroom and trust me, you will be fanning yourself …<br><br><i> <blockquote> “Danika, sweetheart?” He rasped.<br><br>“Yes, Tristan?”<br><br>“I’m done being sweet, if you don’t mind. I’d like to fuck you really hard if that’s okay.” </blockquote></i> <br>But all good things must come to an end. At the end of the day, they were both just so strongly shaped by their past. Tristan couldn’t do commitment and Danika couldn’t do casual and when the hurt came, it HURT. I understood where both of them were coming from but it didn’t stop it from being oh so painful.<br><br>But I loved seeing them work through it. And, as with every other part of their relationship, it was with openness and honesty. Yes, there were some pretty painful, gut-wrenching mistakes made but because of how much I felt I understood what led up to it and because of the way they worked their way back together, I never found myself frustrated with the story. Yes, I swore (out-loud) and I might have face-palmed once or twice but at the same time, I loved it! A lot of it was really about Tristan figuring out what his heart wanted. Everyone makes mistakes and everything about him was just so genuine and sincere that I couldn’t help but forgive everything he did that hurt my heart and Danika’s especially given his profuse and sincere apology. And, to be fair to him, his mistakes were never stupid, they were understandable given his past… they just hurt like fucking hell.<br><br>The ending built in intensity. There were ohhhhhhh FUCK moments, tragic moments and finally happiness.<br><br>There is no relationship cliffhanger at the end but their story is far from over. We are treated to the first chapter of the next book at the end of this one which gives a solid idea of where their story will go. Also, given some of the things we know about their future from Up In The Air, we know they have a rocky road ahead of them but I am so looking forward to seeing them work through it.<br><br>The author has said that she is 99% sure that this will be a 2-book series and she has a whole series of FAQs that I’ve linked at the bottom of the page here. I have come to really trust this author’s writing and I can’t wait to see where she takes their story next.<br><br>Timeline-wise, this book took place before In Flight and we actually get several awesome cameos from James Cavendish (the hero of the Up In The Air series) but in his pre-Bianca days. But it was cool to get to see him in a whole new light because we knew him as the kinky fuckhot lover, but in this book we actually get to see him at work.<br><br>There are no spoilers in this book for the Up In The Air series. I’d really call this a spin-off series. Many of the characters in from the UITA series not only make an appearance, but are main supporting characters in this book but at the same time, you could easily read this as a stand alone. My personal recommendation though would be to read the UITA series in full first. I think you’d get the most complete picture that way but it’s not absolutely necessary.<br><br><b> R.K. Lilley’s writing is addictive, her stories are captivating and you are guaranteed to fall in love with her characters. There is a reason she’s one of my favorite authors! I highly recommend this book! It was an absolutely wonderful read! </b><br><br>4.5 stars!<br><br>Here's my casting (also, see above):<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410623i/805391.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410623i/805392._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410623i/805393._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>******************<br><br><b> QUESTIONS &amp; ANSWERS about this series from the author!! <br><br>Q. Is Bad Things going to be a series?<br><br> A. Yes. Bad Things will be a series, titled Tristan &amp; Danika, and I’m hoping to keep it to two books, both of which will be full length novels.<br><br>Q. Is this a spin-off of the Up in the Air trilogy?<br><br>A. I would call this a connected series, rather than a spin-off. In fact, you could even read it standalone, and if you haven’t read Up in the Air, Bad Things does not have any spoilers for the series, so you could actually read it first. <br><br>Q. Who are Tristan and Danika again? <br><br>A. These characters were introduced in Grounded, but you don’t have to go back and brush up on exactly who they are, if you don’t remember, as this series introduces them anew, in fact it starts at the very beginning of their love story.<br><br>Q. What the f*** happened between Tristan &amp; Danika?<br><br>A. That one I won’t be answering, I’ll be showing, and the answer may surprise you. Their history is a lot more rich and heartbreaking than anyone imagined, and the damage is a lot worse than a limp. <br><br>Q. If I’ve never read one of your books before, could I start with Bad Things?<br><br>A. Absolutely! This book has no spoilers for the others, so you could certainly start with this one. <br><br>Q. Is Bad Things a BDSM series , like Up in the Air?<br><br>A. It is not. There is certainly an element of domination in the dynamic of T&amp;D’s relationship, and there’s kink, even bondage, but not the S&amp;M. That just isn’t who these characters are, or how they relate to each other.<br><br>Q. If you had to pick a favorite, which would it be - James Cavendish or Tristan Vega? <br><br>A. I’d rather pull out all of my hair and shave off my eyebrows than answer that question! I’m totally in love with both of them! <br><br>Q. How long is Bad Things?<br><br>A. I just got the paperback proof, and it is 363 pages!<br><br>Q. When will this book be released on Nook and KOBO?<br><br>A. Bad Things will be available on Amazon, in paperback, Nook, and Kobo on June 11th. It is currently available for pre-order on Amazon and Kobo. <br><br>I’ve also submitted the book for iTunes, but I can’t say when they will make it available, as their review process is arbitrary and drawn-out. </b><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410623i/805394._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>

After having devoured the Up In the Air-series, I was already a fan of author R.K. Lilley, but now I just became an even bigger one. Seriously, if you have not read this book yet, read it ASAP! I assure you, you won't regret it. This book had all the ingredients for it to be an absolute <b>MUST READ</b>.<br><br>I loved Danika's sarcasm and feisty character, Tristan's sexy bad boy-attitude, their playful banter and let's not forget, the "off the charts" HOT sex scenes, including a certain scene on the hood of a car...<br><br><b>

Having been through a dramatic youth and being estranged from her only family members left, she's become an expert at keeping people at a distance. At the age of twenty one, she feels like she has finally found her place in life. She works her way through college by working as a nanny for a family who has become a huge aspect of her life. She has a few close friends and enough chores to keep her busy throughout the week. <br><br>Her life isn't perfect but it's peaceful and in control and that's exactly the way she likes it. In the past, Danika has always fallen for the bad boys who left her feeling heartbroken and empty inside. So, she has decided to stay single for a while and to stay clear any tempting bad boys. But then she meets <b>Tristan Vega</b>, the <i>ultimate</i> bad boy. The moment she meets him, she knows he's trouble with a capital T. And yet, with his irresistible charms, she can't seem to stay away from him.<br><br><b><i>"He smiled his best smile, the one that ruined me for every other smile in the world."</i></b><br><br>Tristan is the perfect charmer; he's sweet, playful and little bit arrogant. Aside from being a club promotor in Vegas, he's also the lead singer of an upcoming band and has women lining up to get a slice of his attention. All in all, he's the ultimate player. Which is why Danika has decided <i>nothing</i> can ever happen between them. He takes her out, and together they start partying almost every night. But, the more time they spend together, the closer they become and the more the sexual tension grows between them. Which sometimes, as a reader, felt like witnessing a train wreck without being able to look away. They love each other and they're pretty much perfect for each other, yet, drama seems to follow them around whenever they're together. They have so much in common, but when it comes to certain matters, they're complete opposites. The question is, will their love be enough or will their differences be their undoing? Because of the beautiful moments they've shared <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I can't help but hope they will get their HEA... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><b><i>"When it's right, like it is with us, it doesn't make your life harder, it makes it better, even when it's hard. I've never been as happy as I've been with you and I don't begin to know how to get past that."</i></b><br><br>A little warning for future readers: during the last few chapters, something happened that I did NOT see coming, something that left me emotional and heartbroken and that even made me shed a few tears.<br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/529352.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Overall, this book was an absolute page-turner for me. Danika and Tristan's story was unique, different, powerful, funny, sexy and at times tragic, which turned out to be the perfect mixture of ingredients to keep me glued to the pages from the moment I started reading it. And although, it did not end with a cliffhanger, I'm already anxiously awaiting the next part of Tristan and Danika's crazy, wild and beautiful love story!<br><br><br><b>♦ <u>MY CASTING</u> ♦</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409943i/803175._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409943i/803176._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></p></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9953335158885269753"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br/><br/>  R.K. Lilley did it again! Now, Tristan was no Mr. Cavendish, but he was pretty damn close. It was intense- sweet, sexy, and an emotional roller coaster, but I loved every minute! <br/><br/>Tristan is a club promoter. He is in a band. He is all kinds of sexy and awesome, but he has commitment issues. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505664853i/23945732.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Danika is working as a live in nanny. She also goes to school full time. Even though she’s only in her early twenties, she is living the life of someone much older. And she ONLY does relationships</span>
  <span id="freeText9953335158885269753" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br><br>  R.K. Lilley did it again! Now, Tristan was no Mr. Cavendish, but he was pretty damn close. It was intense- sweet, sexy, and an emotional roller coaster, but I loved every minute! <br><br>Tristan is a club promoter. He is in a band. He is all kinds of sexy and awesome, but he has commitment issues. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505664853i/23945732.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Danika is working as a live in nanny. She also goes to school full time. Even though she’s only in her early twenties, she is living the life of someone much older. And she ONLY does relationships. No flings, no friends with benefits. EVER. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505664853i/23945733.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Tristan’s needs somewhere to stay for just a week or so, he crashes with Danika’s boss Jerry. Danika knows Tristan is trouble when she first meets him, but she can’t resist his charms. They become fast friends. <br><i>
  <blockquote>‘I’m bad with relationships with women my own age, too, that’s why I don’t do them.’<br><br>‘So what do you do?’<br><br>‘Hookups. Brief, casual hookups. How about you?’<br><br>‘I do relationships. No exceptions. Never had a casual hookup in my life.’<br><br>‘Well, I guess that makes things less complicated. We’ll be friends then.’</blockquote>
</i><br>Tristan knows Danika is special. They spend weeks together, dancing, clubbing, just hanging out and getting to know one another. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Danika was like a breath of fresh air. A breath of fresh air I didn’t get to fuck.</blockquote>
</b> The sexual tension between them builds and builds... Even though they are ‘just friends’ they find it necessary to make a list of rules... <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>THE FRIENDS DON’T LIST:<br>1- No sex, no making out, no kissing.<br>2- No getting jealous or complaining about who the other one is dating or hooking up with.<br>3- We can hang out whenever we want, but we won’t call it a date, even if we’re doing date-like things.<br>4- No nagging<br>5-Always remember we like each other too much to sleep together, and that sleeping together will ruin EVERYTHING.<br>6- If the words ‘I love you’ are ever mentioned, it will be assumed that it is in a friendship type context<br><s>7- No talking dirty, or talking about dates with your vibrator</s>
</blockquote>
</b><br>These rules last... but only for a little while. These two just can’t deny what they have together. They are both falling for one another, even though they don’t want to admit it. <br><br><br>Tristan will do anything to be with Danika- but she has become his best friend. He can’t risk losing her. He won’t. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>‘I want you so badly that I’d do just about anything to have you.’ he said roughly. ‘The only thing I won’t do, though, is risk losing you. Can you promise me that if we do this, I won’t lose you?’</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>So they are able to balance it for a while.<br><b>
  <blockquote>We became passionate lovers and stayed the best of friends.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>These two have chemistry... and let me tell you- it is OFF THE CHARTS! <br><br>Things don’t stay great for long... Danika is falling even harder for Tristan, but he still can’t admit his feelings for her. He has deluded himself to believe that they are just ‘friends with benifits’ and that just doesn’t work for her. He doesn’t know what to do. He wants to be there for her, but he just can’t be what she needs right now. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I’ll always stick around for you, Danika. I mean that. You’re my best friend. No matter what, I’ll always be there for you, if you want me.”</i>
</b><br><br>After making some collosel mistakes, Tristan FINALLY gets it together. He realizes what an idiot he has been and that he needs Danika. He doesn’t need all the other girls. He may not be ready to give her those three little words, but he wants her to forgive him, and let him try to be her boyfriend. A title he hasn’t worn in a very long time. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’ve got no right to ask, but will you give me the chance to prove that I can be better than I’ve been?”<br><br>“I need you. I’ve never needed anyone or anything the way I need you. I need you in a way that would break me if I ever lost you. Being with you makes every part of my life better. Every second I get with you is the best second of my life. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>  If you have read R.K. Lilley’s ‘Up In the Air’ trilogy, you know that this woman knows how to write a sex scene! This book was freakin’ HOT! Smokin’ hot! Tristan was sexy, dominate, and some of the things that came out of his mouth had me fanning myself. Seriously! <br><br>Once Danika and Tristan are ‘together’ it is NOT all rainbows and sunshine. They have a lot of obstacles and difficulties. I swooned, I smiled, I laughed, I cried like a baby <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[OMG poor Jared- I about lost it!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br>Tristan was one of the sweetest, most charming and sexy leading men. Sure, he was a commitmaphobe with some manwhoroish ways- but I adored this guy! He will make you swoon! Danika was strong, funny and sassy. I really enjoyed her character as well.<br><br>This story was amazing. Just wonderful. I also LOVED the cameo’s from my very own Mr. Beautiful- James Cavendish. Just so everyone knows, there is NO CLIFFHANGER! But I am extremely nervous to see what is going to transpire in the second book. From seeing where these two end up in ‘Mile High’, I’m biting my nails just waiting for the fall out. Lets hope book 2 comes out soon! A great 5 star read :D<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I see now that I didn’t know a thing about love before I met you. When it’s right, like it is with us, it doesn’t make your life harder, it makes your life better even when its hard.”</blockquote>
</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer645301253" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17183375365699375512"><b>Full review posted</b><br/><br/><b>4 CONSUMING but EXHAUSTING stars!</b><br/><br/><b>HOLY COW! I'm mentally EXHAUSTED!</b> I wasn't prepared for such an angsty, emotional, and gut-wrenching story. In fact, I felt it became a bit over-the-top with the all angst and drama toward the end. However, I was completely spellbound and consumed while reading this book. <br/><br/>Where this story really shined for me was in the <b>writing, characterization and chemistry between the two main leads</b>. It was <b>exceptional</b>. In fact, I'm not sure I've read a book </span>
  <span id="freeText17183375365699375512" style="display:none"><b>Full review posted</b><br /><br /><b>4 CONSUMING but EXHAUSTING stars!</b><br /><br /><b>HOLY COW! I'm mentally EXHAUSTED!</b> I wasn't prepared for such an angsty, emotional, and gut-wrenching story. In fact, I felt it became a bit over-the-top with the all angst and drama toward the end. However, I was completely spellbound and consumed while reading this book. <br /><br />Where this story really shined for me was in the <b>writing, characterization and chemistry between the two main leads</b>. It was <b>exceptional</b>. In fact, I'm not sure I've read a book that had better characterization or character chemistry.<br /><br />This book revolves solely around Tristan (LOVE his name) and Danika's feelings and relationship.They had incredible chemistry right from the start–which made for scorching hot, passionate love scenes–and I was quickly drawn into their topsy-turvily world. <br /><br />I <b>LOVED</b> both Tristan's and Danika's characters. Tristan is your typical jaded-by-love bad boy whose man-whoring ways left much to be desired in my opinion (I hated that aspect of the plot and his character). But, boy, did he <b>sweep me off my feet with his dimpled smile and off-the-chart charisma</b>. As for Danika...well...she was simply fantastic. I adored her. I sympathized with her. I cried and laughed with her. And I understood her. <b>I lived this book through her eyes and went on the gut-wrenching roller coaster ride that was Tristan with her.</b><br /><br />My only true beef with this story– other than wishing the author would have include their whole story in one long book instead of two–was the excessive drama and angst...especially toward the end. Other than that, I thoroughly loved reading this book. Angst exhaustion and all. <br /><br />Note: Even though this book isn't the last of Tristan and Danika's story, it does end with a HEA. Thank heavens for that!!!</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer4964116709170673184"><b>FOUR.5 TRISTAN STARS.</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"I fell apart and came back together again, my whole world thoroughly rocked."</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395409985i/8992006._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Welcome to 'Bad Things' a novel that combines easy reading and combustible in one addictive story. A tale about a love that is as much messy as it is meant to be. R K Lilley's books are a reading habit that I don't want to break anytime soon. I loved the 'in flight' series, James Cavendish is more than a little unforgettable, so it goes without saying that I was more than looking forward to wha</span>
  <span id="freeText4964116709170673184" style="display:none"><b>FOUR.5 TRISTAN STARS.</b><br><br><i>
  <b>"I fell apart and came back together again, my whole world thoroughly rocked."</b>

A tale about a love that is as much messy as it is meant to be. R K Lilley's books are a reading habit that I don't want to break anytime soon. I loved the 'in flight' series, James Cavendish is more than a little unforgettable, so it goes without saying that I was more than looking forward to what 'Bad things' would deliver.<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>Along with her therapists help, friends advice and a drink or two, Danika has sworn of the perpetual bad boy. Having two failed relationships that would make a car crash look pretty, Danika is determined she will stay single. only problem is she has been labelled as a love addict and Tristan Vega has just walked into her life. Tristan is a jack of all trades, hardworking playboy. relationships are certainly not his thing, so when he encounters Danika, a friend who more than meets his match this bad boy feels like breaking the rules. With secrets well hidden and hearts on the line can this duo make it to the end or will what brought them together force them apart.<br><br><b>The characters ...</b><br>Tristan Vega is utterly delicious, charismatic, charming and described to bad boy perfection, not to mention he also has the tattoos and dimples to match. I can say without doubt that this character has hit my top five, he has spades of goodness but the package doesn't come without fault, this charmer has commitment failure written all over him along with some serious anger management issues, it's a rocky journey from start to finish with this gorgeous bad boy.<br><br>Danika is a book sweetheart, sassy confident and utterly likeable, she's as much beautiful as she is attracted to the wrong man. A character who is easy to fall for but has a large case of the needy girlfriend factor, with a loveless past and heartbreaking upbringing this character needs more than words to reassure her fragile heart.<br><br><b>What I loved ... </b><br>This author has a wicked talent for writing the most scrumptious male characters. I'm suggesting good reads has it own Oscar ceremony and RK Lilley should win best prize for creating these addictive male counterparts. That's not forgetting that she also creates a platform for a loveable heroine - hooray, this makes me one happy reader. The chemistry was I.N.S.A.N.E what this author can't create with words in a standoff between lovers ain't worth thinking about. One word to sum up this novel? (yes you guessed) H.O.T I enjoyed the push and pull of the fractious relationship. Best sexual tension in a book EVER, I seriously thought my kindle was going to spontaneously combust. 'Bad things' is a mix of intoxicating passion and a whole lot of failure to commit, it almost had it all for me but I couldn't commit to the full five so with that being said ..<br><br><b>Why not five?</b><br>Straight up this book was a five star read for me right up till about 70% mark then the double standards and immaturity started to come into play. I found myself irritated with both Tristan and Danika and it took the five star shine off for me. It's a HUGE shame that the last 30% rattled my rating, but don't be mislead by my 'why not five' this book is worth a read I'm sure you'll fall in book love.<br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>If you loved RK Lilly's In Flight series then this is not to be missed. If you like a story with a troubled love vibe then this will hit the spot. Great characters, plenty of hot and spicy and it also has a sneaky peek back to some of our favourite characters from the in flight series. You like the sound of this? Go get it readers ...</span>

Lilley fangirlie, then you’re probably already a little familiar with Tristan and Danika. We’ve had a few teasing hints of their story in the Up In The Air Trilogy. We know that they were not speaking to each other, that Danika limps and this has something to do with Tristan and that she has forgiven him but is unable to forget what has happened in the past. It’s all very mysterious and we begin this one years before when Danika is just twenty-one and they meet for the very first time.<br><br> <br>Danika is instantly attracted to Tristan but he makes it clear that he is only into random hook ups with women and doesn’t do relationships. They get on so well together and agree to be best friends and never allow a sexual relationship to damage that relationship. They mean a lot to one another and, despite the deep attraction they both feel, agree to just be friends and even make a list of rules to abide by.<br><br>Danika is such a sweetheart – she’s refreshingly honest, sarcastic, sassy, a fantastic dancer and is like a breath of fresh air to Tristan who is used to false, fake women. She’s had a hard and challenging childhood that’s shaped the way she feels about relationships today. She just wants to belong to someone and for them to belong to her, to be loved in a way that one one has ever loved her. They spark up an incredible friendship and start to mean so much to one another that they fear that their sexual attraction will ruin it and Tristan is desperate not to lose her.<br><br><br>Well, R.K. He makes a lot of mistakes but he’s big enough to admit when he’s wrong and realise how important Danika has become to him.<br><br>I really enjoyed this book – it’s so very sexy and charming. I fell a lot in love with Tristan possibly even more than Mr Cavendish and I adored him.     <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537321453?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537321453" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18411246321558480321"><b>
  <i>"Bad things were going to happen if we spent too much time around each other."</i>
</b><br/><br/>That's what Danika thought when she first met Tristan and she wasn't exactly wrong. She has always been attracted to bad boys but they are bad news for her. On top of that, Tristan only does hook ups and Danika only does relationships so her and Tristan decide to just be friends. And that really is for the best because they've both been through a lot in the past. <br/><br/>If you read the <i>Up in the Air</i> series, you've met Tri</span>
  <span id="freeText18411246321558480321" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Bad things were going to happen if we spent too much time around each other."</i>
</b><br><br>That's what Danika thought when she first met Tristan and she wasn't exactly wrong. She has always been attracted to bad boys but they are bad news for her. On top of that, Tristan only does hook ups and Danika only does relationships so her and Tristan decide to just be friends. And that really is for the best because they've both been through a lot in the past. <br><br>If you read the <i>Up in the Air</i> series, you've met Tristan and Danika and you what know what's going on with them...well, a little. This is what happens <i>before</i> so you don't need to read that series to read this one. <br><br>That being said, <b>READ THIS BOOK!</b> Holy Awesomesauce...sooo good. Tristan is yummy, Danika is feisty, the sex is AMAZING, it's emotional and of course, there's lots of drama! Another book that just sucked me in and I couldn't put it down. <br><br>Tristan...WOW! and what's weird is that I didn't feel that way reading the <i>Up in the Air</i> series, obviously because of how Danika is in that series and that's what just reeled me in. What could possibly have happened? He is a Rock Star, Sex God, can cook like no other, women, animals and kids love him, and he has dimples, muscles and tattoos, oh my!...the list goes on and on. Unfortunately, he does have some faults...and they are doozies! But it was wonderful getting some chapters in his POV. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582145.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love Danika! I'm sorry to keep saying this but if you've read the <i>Up in the Air</i> series, your heart goes out to her. She's a fighter though so you know it had be to something serious and it's just <i>killing me</i> to not know! UGH! I do love that she finally took a chance on Tristan and is living in the moment and letting go of being so in control. <br><br>Tristan + Danika = <b>HOT STUFF!</b> I just can't say that enough...you have to read this just to read the sex scenes!! ;) Let's just leave it at...<i>anywhere and anytime</i>!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379793741i/582146._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are a lot of great characters in the story...I especially loved Tristan's brother, Jared, and Frankie, whom we've met from...you guessed it, the <i>Up in the Air</i> series. We didn't get a lot of Frankie in that series though so it was great getting to know her better. Of course, lovely Mr. Cavendish makes several appearances. (You may get a little, slight spoiler about him if you read this book first but it's nothing you won't find out fairly early in his series.)<br><br>Some of the drama is over the top...and excessive. I felt like both Danika and Tristan weren't learning from their mistakes. And I was a little disappointed at Danika's change of behavior in the last half of the book. There's also a major scene that happens towards the end and to be honest, I'm not really sure the reasoning's behind it. <br><br>There is no cliffhanger...the story is just unfinished. Thankfully, we do get an excerpt of the next book, <i>Rock Bottom</i>, which had even more drama! And the title is a little <i>scary</i> but I still can't wait!<br><br><br>Favorite quotes: <br><br>♦ "On behalf of men everywhere, thank you for wearing sexy f*cking shoes. I’ll try to remember not to walk too fast.”<br><br>♦ “All I heard just now was ‘blah, blah, blah Danika wins’.”<br><br>♥ "Were you taking your own version of a ‘shower’ in there?”<br><br>♥ <b>“I’m going to f*ck you hard on the hood of this car, in the pouring rain. And. You. Are. Not. Going. To. Forget. It.”</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="18411246321558480321" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_637668100" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637668100" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637668100?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637668100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13781470327020640302"><b>4.5 super hot, rollicking stars!</b><br/><br/>Considering how I disliked R.K. Lilley's Up in the Series, I wasn't expecting much of anything going into this book. But color me surprised, I actually ended up loving it. <br/><br/>Yes, it was angsty, both the MCs annoyed at me at some point, some of the drama were a bit juvenile, and yet, I really enjoyed the whole thing. To me this has an entirely different feel than Up in the Air series and I find Danika and Tristan's story more relatable, more gritty and more raw than </span>
  <span id="freeText13781470327020640302" style="display:none"><b>4.5 super hot, rollicking stars!</b><br><br>Considering how I disliked R.K. Lilley's Up in the Series, I wasn't expecting much of anything going into this book. But color me surprised, I actually ended up loving it. <br><br>Yes, it was angsty, both the MCs annoyed at me at some point, some of the drama were a bit juvenile, and yet, I really enjoyed the whole thing. To me this has an entirely different feel than Up in the Air series and I find Danika and Tristan's story more relatable, more gritty and more raw than Up in the Air. In other, I was totally engrossed and invested in their story. <br><br><u>Tristan</u><br><a href="http://imgur.com/sd1Rh5G" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424830i/847174.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tristan was a super-hot, tattooed, bad boy, club promoter/rock star with a wicked sense of humor. I loved his sense of humor especially when he was with Danika. But beneath all that was a troubled young man. I felt that in this book, we barely scratched the surface of who Tristan truly is. And as we have seen from Grounded, he definitely went to hell and back. <br><br>I loved the fact that he was flawed. I felt it added to the complexity of his character. I mean, he did some things that were just terrible. TERRIBLE. And he hurt Danika real bad. But the readers also get to see his vulnerable side especially when it comes to his relationship with Danika and his family. <br><br><u>Danika</u><br><a href="http://imgur.com/JDG6Y1t" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424830i/847175._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Danika hasn't had an easy life. She had a shitty childhood and because of this, she has some self-esteem issues, not to mention she seemed to be attracted to guys who are totally wrong for her. When she met Tristan, she can't deny her attraction to him but she knows he could be very bad for her. She knows it but she can't seem to help herself anyway. <br><br><u>Their Relationship</u><br><a href="http://imgur.com/5N7njbu" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411755ra/809271.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>At the onset, Tristan was attracted to Danika and vice versa. I was glad this wasn't some case of insta-lust or inta-love. Yes, the attraction was there but they didn't immediately act on it, which is probably why I liked this book in the first place. See, Tristan doesn't do relationships. He's content with casual hook-ups. On the other hand, Danika doesn't do hook-ups or anything casual. She's a relationship kind of girl. See the dilemma there? <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I know. Just too old to be dating eighteen-year olds, or even twenty-one year olds. Frankly, though, I’m bad with women my own age, too, when it comes to relationships, which is why I don’t do them.”<br><br> I couldn’t help it. I had to ask. “So what do you do?”<br><br> “Hookups. Brief, casual hookups. How about you?”<br><br> I shook my head, pursing my lips at him. I couldn’t quite believe that we had jumped to this already. He was a man to be careful of, to be sure. “I do relationships. No exceptions. Never had a casual hookup in my life.”<br><br> He sighed, measuring some flour into the mixing bowl. “Well, I guess that makes things less complicated. We’ll be friends, then.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>Easier said than done. They fought their attraction to each other, ignored their chemistry, all for the sake of their friendship. They even made a "Friends Don't List" to protect themselves from each other. Yeah, like that would work. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/uTPGdT9" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424830ra/847176.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>To make the long story short, the Friends Don't List was an epic failure. Of course, they just had to get to together. As a reader, I was happy when they finally got together. I mean, it was inevitable but this is when bad things really started to happen. Bad, bad things. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/s5QNGtU" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424830ra/847177.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Halfway through, I was crying ugly tears, I was mad at Tristan, I wanted to strangle Dean and throw my Kindle across the room at the same time. OTT, I know but this book had seriously put me through the ringer. And just when I thought, all the drama is finally over, the rug got pulled under my feet. Something bad happened to Tristan's family member, which was really, really sad and really, really made me cry. I wasn't expecting that, which made it all the more sad. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/JPAmnaR" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424589ra/846531.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anyway, I can't wait for the next book. There wasn't really any cliffhanger here. The book did end with Danika and Tristan together. But for those of you who have read Grounded, you know some very bad things are in store for these two. So yeah, can't wait for more angst the second time around. <br><br>Before I forget. I know you're all dying to know. Well, this book...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/u4ItdZR" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424830ra/847178.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/OPQdbP8" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424830ra/847179.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Peace out!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13781470327020640302" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11960649787000561385"><br/>Saw some good reviews for this one here and decided to give it a go. Was not disappointed. I really enjoyed it. As one reviewer said, it flowed. Tristan Vega, very nice indeed. Tough Rock Star. Danika, bit messed up by her past – They are friends but can they stay just friends. Don’t think so, their attraction is too hard to resist.     </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537425485" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6702462647339634361"><b> OKAY! </b> I have been waiting on this book since forever it seems... and I'm happy to report that the wait was so worth it. I give it 4.5 stars but I bumped it up for rating purposes. Bad Things tells the story of how Danika and Tristan, who we are introduced to in the Up In The Air Trilogy, met and proceeded to fall in love. <br/><br/>First off this shit is H-O-T!!!!! Like change your panties multiple times kind of hot. It takes them awhile to get to that part of it but once they do...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/667056.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote> <b> "I don't want this </b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6702462647339634361" style="display:none"><b> OKAY! </b> I have been waiting on this book since forever it seems... and I'm happy to report that the wait was so worth it. I give it 4.5 stars but I bumped it up for rating purposes. Bad Things tells the story of how Danika and Tristan, who we are introduced to in the Up In The Air Trilogy, met and proceeded to fall in love. <br><br>First off this shit is H-O-T!!!!! Like change your panties multiple times kind of hot. It takes them awhile to get to that part of it but once they do...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/667056.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> "I don't want this to be calculated for you... I want you to let go. I want you to submit. I want to make you lose your mind. I want you to be so far gone that the only word left in your vocabulary is my name." </b> </blockquote><br><br><blockquote> <b> "I know what you taste like..." </b> </blockquote><br><br><blockquote> <b> "I'm going to fuck you on the hood of this car, in the pouring rain. And. You. Are. Not. Going. To. Forget. It." </b> </blockquote><br><br>There is absolutely no doubt that these two are in love and well before either one of them is willing to admit it - we know it! They are comfortable with and insanely attracted to each other from day 1. They quickly become one of the <b> CRAZIEST </b> couples ever... in life! They are both ridiculously jealous, possessive, they are fearful of each others feelings and their own. They fight and say crappy ass shit to each other and they both have had a shit start in life to overcome. Through it all though you will never doubt that these two are so very much in love and even though they may be bad for each other at times you can't help but to route for them. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409848ra/802872.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>We get to see Tristan trying to make a name for himself and Danika trying to figure out her purpose in life. We by no means get a resolution to any of that in this first book but we definitely get a good foundation for where they end up in the Up In The Air Trilogy. Mr. Beautiful himself makes a few appearances as well. <b> *Swoon* </b> Just like in the Up In The Air Trilogy the supporting characters were also dynamic and easy to get invested in as well. <br><br><br><br>This review may be just a tad bit biased because I have a total lady boner for R.K. Lilley... but I promise you it doesn't matter if I do kiss the ground that an author walks on, if it wasn't good I would keep it real with you. I cannot wait for the next book in this series especially because of where and how we find this couple in the Up In The Air trilogy - I'm a little nervous as to what this next book will bring. I truly hope though that they get their HEA!!! Be prepared to swoon, throw things, laugh, cry, and cream reading this one folks!!!! <br><br><br><b> My Tristan </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409849i/802873._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409849i/802874._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b> My Danika </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409849i/802875.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17360780671683079813"><b>
  <i>His kiss was insidious, seeping into every part of me. He took me over in a way I couldn't believe I allowed. A few seconds into the kiss, and I was ready to relinquish all control, which I'd have sworn was the antithesis of everything I was before I'd met Tristan.</i>

  <span id="freeText17360780671683079813" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>His kiss was insidious, seeping into every part of me. He took me over in a way I couldn't believe I allowed. A few seconds into the kiss, and I was ready to relinquish all control, which I'd have sworn was the antithesis of everything I was before I'd met Tristan.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410432i/804682.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I knew we were going to be a dangerous combination. Bad things were going to happen if we spent too much time around each other.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410432i/804683._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book! Sweet baby Jebus, THIS BOOK! I was not expecting to be as good as it was or to suck me into the story as it did. <br><br>Danika has a penchant for picking bad boys. So when she meets Tristan, whose sexy body, dimples and tattoos practically scream out bad, the icing on the cake is he's also in a band. She is determined to keep him at a distance. But as they say, the road to hell is paved with good intentions.<br><br>Danika and Tristan start out as friends. Tristan is determined to show her a more exciting life than what he sees her currently leading.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410432ra/804684.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>In the intoxicating mist of Vegas nightlife, drinks, and sexual tension, they begin to get closer.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410432ra/804685.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Danika's reference to being drunk as "feeling pretty". She had some of the funniest lines in this book.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"I named my vibrator after you," I told him with a smirk. "He's small, but he makes up for it by working hard.</b>
</blockquote><br>The sexual tension between these two is scorching. But after one failing relationship after another, Danika is determined to be single, and Tristan just doesn't do relationships. They can only ignore what's igniting between them for so long...<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Tell me not to kiss you," he said, when his lips were a breath away from mine.<br>"Don't kiss me," I told him, my voice a breathless rasp.<br>"Mean it."<br>"I can't," I gasped. </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410432ra/804686.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And it's not long before a few stolen kisses start to give way to more desperate passions.<br><br>This book had one of the hottest non-sex scenes I have ever read. </blockquote></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer639883127" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9651743412735042294"><b>Nothing sucked worse than having feelings for someone who just may have been your best friend. Especially when that someone clearly didn’t return those feelings.</b><br/><br/>Two words…<b>HOT DAMN!</b> I don’t think I’ve ever read a book with more intense sexual chemistry between the two main characters. I could actually feel the heat coming off of these two. As an added bonus we’re treated to an actual story, too. <br/><br/><b>Danika was like a breath of fresh air. A breath of fresh air that I didn’t get to fuck.</b><br/><br/>Danika doesn’t </span>
  <span id="freeText9651743412735042294" style="display:none"><b>Nothing sucked worse than having feelings for someone who just may have been your best friend. Especially when that someone clearly didn’t return those feelings.</b><br /><br />Two words…<b>HOT DAMN!</b> I don’t think I’ve ever read a book with more intense sexual chemistry between the two main characters. I could actually feel the heat coming off of these two. As an added bonus we’re treated to an actual story, too. <br /><br /><b>Danika was like a breath of fresh air. A breath of fresh air that I didn’t get to fuck.</b><br /><br />Danika doesn’t do casual hookups and Tristan never does relationships. The attraction between them is immediate but so is the mutual respect and the fact that they actually really <i>like</i> one another. What are two smokin’ hot people who are wildly attracted to one another but don’t see eye to eye on relationships to do? They immediately agree to keep things just friends only. They even draw up a cute little list of the do’s and don’ts of their relationship in order to make sure things stay nice and friend-like:<br /><br /><b> 1. No sex, no making out, no kissing.<br /> 2. No getting jealous or complaining about who the other one is dating or hooking up with.<br /> 3. We can hang out whenever we want, but we won’t call it a date, even if we’re doing date- like things<br /> 4. No nagging.<br /> 5. Always remember that we like each other too much to sleep together, and that sleeping <br /> together will ruin EVERYTHING.<br /> 6. If the words ‘I love you’ are ever mentioned, it will be assumed that it is in a friendship type context<br /> 7. No talking dirty, or talking about dates with your vibrator.</b><br /><br />Seems simple enough. Except it’s not. The more time they spend together, the more items on the list get thrown out the window.<br /><br /><b>”I want you so badly that I’d do just about anything to have you,” he said roughly. “The only thing I won’t do, though, is risk losing you. Can you promise me that if we do this, I won’t lose you?”<br />I didn’t hesitate, didn’t think over the question as I should have. I wanted him, and I wanted him now. “I promise.”</b><br /><br />I loved this book and not just for the sexy stuff. Both characters were written so well and I felt like I knew them after the story ended.<b> And there was an actual story!</b> I like smut as much as the next gal but I’m really tired of reading sex scene after sex scene with nothing else to go along with it. I get bored, start braiding my hair and think about how I’m not doing enough for that whole world peace deal and the story’s lost to me. <i>Bad Things</i> absolutely captured my attention the entire time and by the end I’d laughed, cried and felt a little sick with worry about what’s in store for these two in the future. What I do know for certain is that I can’t freaking WAIT to find out!</span>

</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/qXaWhMJ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413543i/814417.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One final note… did I get tingly inside when I realized Danika is half Asian, maybe, but what?! It’s the little things I look for in a read and THANK YOU for that! <br><br><b>
  <i>He tipped my chin up with a finger, then slanted his mouth over mine. Right in the middle of Costco. I thought it was the sweetest thing in the world.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Lbe6rql" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413543i/814418.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For more reviews, visit <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline's Reads</a><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_" title="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1371404883s/17377032.jpg" alt="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00CX3F2QY/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00CX3F2QY&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00CX3F2QY/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00CX3F2QY&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10149567231197764097"><b>STEAMY!</b><br/>My kindle was emitting smoke as I read <b>Bad Things</b>. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Bad things were going to happen if we spent too much time around each other.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><b>Danika</b> and <b>Tristan</b> meet through a mutual friend. From the moment they met the sexual tension was high. When these two hook up it's off the charts. Trust issues hinders their relationship around every corner.<blockquote>
<i><b>"I see now that I didn't know a thing about love before I met you. When it's right, like it is with us, it doesn't make your life harder, it makes</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10149567231197764097" style="display:none"><b>STEAMY!</b><br>My kindle was emitting smoke as I read <b>Bad Things</b>. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Bad things were going to happen if we spent too much time around each other.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b>Danika</b> and <b>Tristan</b> meet through a mutual friend. From the moment they met the sexual tension was high. When these two hook up it's off the charts. Trust issues hinders their relationship around every corner.<blockquote>
<i><b>"I see now that I didn't know a thing about love before I met you. When it's right, like it is with us, it doesn't make your life harder, it makes your life better, even when it's hard."</b></i> -Tristan</blockquote><br>Thankfully <b>Bad Things</b> doesn't end with a cliffhanger. Looking forward to continuing with Tristan and Danika in the next two books. <br><br>*********************************************************<br> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/105659-tristan-danika" rel="nofollow noopener"><u>Tristan &amp; Danika</u> series</a> is interconnected with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/90780-up-in-the-air" rel="nofollow noopener"><u>Up in the Air</u> series</a>. Each series can be read as a standalone series. <br><br><u>Timeline between the two series:</u><br><i>{#1 T&amp;A} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_" title="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. <div id="review_537341409" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537341409" />
    <a title="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer"><img alt="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363047769p2/10459827.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537341409?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" href="/user/show/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer">Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=tatts">tatts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=leave-me-speechless">leave-me-speechless</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=dreaded-cliffhangers">dreaded-cliffhangers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=hot-in-here">hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=sexy-bad-boy">sexy-bad-boy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537341409" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2938084354736966736">Re-read Review March 22, 13<br/>Just as good as the first time. Love Tristan and Danika and I can't wait to read the rest of the series. :) <br/><br/>Initial Review July 20, 13<br/><b>
  <i>"I knew that we were going to be a dangerous combination. Bad things were going to happen if we spent too much time around each other."</i>
</b><br/><br/>I have soo many emotions right now. That ending just made me a hot mess. I have so much to say, but just can't seem to get it out....<br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/413237.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>The ending has left me.. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409834ra/802837.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/388900.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay I'll try. This is a spin-off from th</span>
  <span id="freeText2938084354736966736" style="display:none">Re-read Review March 22, 13<br>Just as good as the first time. Love Tristan and Danika and I can't wait to read the rest of the series. :) <br><br>Initial Review July 20, 13<br><b>
  <i>"I knew that we were going to be a dangerous combination. Bad things were going to happen if we spent too much time around each other."</i>
</b><br><br>I have soo many emotions right now. That ending just made me a hot mess. I have so much to say, but just can't seem to get it out....<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/413237.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The ending has left me.. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409834ra/802837.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/388900.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay I'll try. This is a spin-off from the Up In the Air series. I have been completely stoked to read this. So freaking excited. This story starts off prior to Bianca and James, even before James knew Tristan. Danika is working for Bev and Jerry. To me the coolest bosses ever. She's their nanny, but once she met Tristan she didn't do a whole lot of that, yet never got in trouble, lol. I'm just saying!! But, I'm getting ahead of myself. The day she meets Tristan she automatically senses that something about him is going to change her entire life. She was not wrong.<br><br>My Tristan<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409834i/802838.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"I want you so badly that I'd do just about anything to have you. The only thing I won't do, though, is risk losing you. Can you promise me that if we do this, I won't lose you?"</i>
</b><br><br>Tristan doesn't do relationships. You'll find out why during the story, but instantly he and Danika both are insanely attracted to each other. But they form a fast friendship and deep connection, so much so that they realize they would rather do anything than to hurt it. Which results in Tristan believing rules need to be made so no lines are crossed that would harm their friendship. <br><br>Danika<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409834i/802839.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"You have me. I'm yours, and I'm not going anywhere, not ever."</i>
</b><br><br>Of course like all rules, it seemed like the instant they were written they both had trouble not breaking them. As Danika says it almost made it seem like a challenge. Once one line is crossed they all begin to be and once they give into their attraction they can't seem to get enough of each other. It was so good, mmmm mmmm. But, remember Tristan doesn't do relationships so once he realizes Danika is seeing this different than what he thinks it is, everything starts to unravel. I literally could go on and on and on, about this book but, hey, I don't want to ruin it for those of you who haven't read it yet.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Tell me not to kiss you." he said when his lips were a breath away from mine. <br>"Don't kiss me," I told him, my voice a breathless rasp.<br>"Mean it," he said, crowing me into the corner of the pool.<br>"I can't," I gasped.<br>The words had barely left my lips before he was kissing me.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409834i/802840.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I felt like my emotions went everywhere with this book. From the sexual frustration between them, to the the hot things Tristan did to Danika and the things he said to her while he was doing them, to blissful happiness, to complete utter tragedy, my emotions were on a whirlwind.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409834ra/802841.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409834i/802842._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tristan was like the best guy ever. Holy cow, I was head over heels in love with him. His restraint, confidence, protectiveness, and his complete understanding, not to mention all of those hot showers, ahaha.<br><br><b>
  <i>"What do you do to food to make it taste this good?" I moaned. <br>I opened my eyes when he didn't answer me. He was staring at me with a look in his eyes that made me toes start to curl. He set down the uneaten half of his sandwich, striding out of the kitchen.<br>"Where are you going?" I called to him.<br>"I'll be back in five minutes," he called back. <br>I wasn't sure if I was pleased or appalled when I heard my shower turning on.</i>
</b><br><br> And dang, I woke up this morning hoping he was in my kitchen cooking me breakfast, sigh, what a disappointment when he wasn't. And then Danika, was so witty. I loved her sarcasm. But I agree, I think she needed to get out and have some fun with Tristan and his buddies. But towards the end, it felt like they just lost control of themselves. Don't worry, I still loved it and it's still going to be 5 stars, it just seemed like they became over possessive, over jealous and always jumped to conclusions in a dramatic form without even beginning to see the whole picture. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409834i/802843._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love love loved Frankie and Jared!! But oh how I hate Dean. HATE HATE HATE him. This is for you Mean Dean, and I think it's only going to get worse in the next book, if that's possible...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409834ra/802844.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But the ending was just so painful. OMG, I had been warned there was a cliffhanger, but I never dreamed this. It wasn't the worse cliffhanger I've ever read, it's just the way it ended. Leaving you wanting more desperately but being too depressed at the same time. If you've read it you know what I mean. I absolutely can NOT wait for the next book in this series. <br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2938084354736966736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
