<span id="freeTextContainer8437814809834465551">Oh my shit...<br/><br/>What an aggravating and agonizing book...<br/><br/>Now, I love me some angsty shit, but here, (mind all the push and pull 'we're just friends and i don't want to ruin that with sex' crap, they still have sex but they are fighting with labels) and now, I'm getting to the point-I fucking can't stand STUPIDITY!!! <br/><br/>I honestly have zero tolerance for human stupidity, especially when all the actions based on that very same stupidity end with lines like: 'I'm sorry, I'm fucked up' or 'I didn't mean t</span>
  <span id="freeText8437814809834465551" style="display:none">Oh my shit...<br /><br />What an aggravating and agonizing book...<br /><br />Now, I love me some angsty shit, but here, (mind all the push and pull 'we're just friends and i don't want to ruin that with sex' crap, they still have sex but they are fighting with labels) and now, I'm getting to the point-I fucking can't stand STUPIDITY!!! <br /><br />I honestly have zero tolerance for human stupidity, especially when all the actions based on that very same stupidity end with lines like: 'I'm sorry, I'm fucked up' or 'I didn't mean that, I'm wired that way' but he still does it anyway...<br /><br />What does that even mean? 'I'm wired that way, I'm fucked up', seems to me that some lame dense excuse to act like a fuckwat asshole instead of owning your shit and man-up!<br /><br />And let me tell you smth about being 'wired that way' since you have no idea what it's like to endure a bloody eruption from one's vayay every month, then suffer some heavy deep hormonal slap from PMS and what?! You have like a solid week or so to actually feel as yourself!! So, the next time I go on killing angry spree I ll fuckin say with a shrug: 'I'm just WIRED that way', asshole!!!<br /><br />I'm digressing here...<br /><br />Back to the story...<br /><br />I mean, wtf?! Either you wanna be with the girl or you fuckin don't wanna be with her...fuckin other chicks after you have a fight with a girl you want but you are too dickwat coward to say it or act on it...well, sorry you are a piece of shit in my eyes, and i don't fucking care about you past, you either fuckin talk and communicate or just fuck the fuck off!!!!<br /><br />And leave the girl alone to make a piece with herself...<br /><br />Jesus, for the ever loving fuck...I have zero tolerance for blunt manwhore fuckers that are coward enough to pull of a 'broken by a past relationship' shit...even if they come clean and get their shit together in the end...<br /><br />Well, fuck off, anyway...<br /><br />2 stars for the heroine...even though, she pissed me off by giving him the chance in the first place...</span>

<div id="review_681425815" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/681425815" />
    <a title="Mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22667925-mia"><img alt="Mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406604077p2/22667925.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/681425815?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mia" href="/user/show/22667925-mia">Mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=forever-favs">forever-favs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22667925-mia?shelf=reread-worthy">reread-worthy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer681425815" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4027640956338328439"><b> 5 stars!!</b><br/><br/>I freaking love this series! This was a re-read and I can honestly say I enjoyed it just as much as the first time. <br/><br/>Anyone who enjoyed the In flight series needs to pick this up, ASAP. We met Tristan and Danika in Grounded, and I instantly wanted to know what was up with these interesting characters that obviously carried lots of history, baggage and tension between them.. I was not surprised the slightest bit when RK announced a spin-off series with Tristan and Danika. <br/><br/>What did surpri</span>
  <span id="freeText4027640956338328439" style="display:none"><b> 5 stars!!</b><br><br>I freaking love this series! This was a re-read and I can honestly say I enjoyed it just as much as the first time. <br><br>Anyone who enjoyed the In flight series needs to pick this up, ASAP. We met Tristan and Danika in Grounded, and I instantly wanted to know what was up with these interesting characters that obviously carried lots of history, baggage and tension between them.. I was not surprised the slightest bit when RK announced a spin-off series with Tristan and Danika. <br><br>What did surprise me what how hard I fell for these characters! Danika, Tristan, Frankie, Jared –I love them all! I didn't expect anything to hold a candle to the In flight series, but RK Lilley completely blew me away with this one.<br><br>Danika and Tristan are so well written and have so much <b>CHEMISTRY</b>. Their story completely draws you in. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394303557ra/8833545.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Danika knew Tristan Vega was Trouble -with a capital <b>T</b>- from the first time she laid eyes on him, but little did she know what she was getting into... <br><br>This wasn't insta-love like so many eroticas lately nor was it cheesy long term best friends secretly in love with each other kinda book... it was a good ol' strangers to friends to lovers type romance. It felt so organic, was so fun and easy to read, Danika and Tristan are definitely my all time favourite dysfunctional lovers. <br><br>So, Tristan doesn't do relationships and Danika doesn't do hookups. So they decide to be “friends”. Neither can deny their crazy attraction so they come up with some rules…<br><br><b> THE FRIENDS DON’T LIST:<br><i>-Because I like you too much to sleep with you-</i><br><blockquote>1- No sex, no making out, no kissing.<br>2- No getting jealous or complaining about who the other one is dating or hooking up with.<br>3- We can hang out whenever we want, but we won’t call it a date, even if we’re doing date-like things.<br>4- No nagging<br>5-Always remember we like each other too much to sleep together, and that sleeping together will ruin EVERYTHING.<br>6- If the words ‘I love you’ are ever mentioned, it will be assumed that it is in a friendship type context<br><s>7- No talking dirty, or talking about dates with your vibrator</s> </blockquote></b><br>This lasts… for a while.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394303557ra/8833546.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But less than a month later:<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “It wasn’t a don’t list, you douche bag, it may as well have been a fucking check-list!” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Tristan and Danika's banter is cute and witty, and had me laughing out loud again and agian. The sexual tension was FIRE. <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Tell me not to kiss you,” he said.<br>“Don’t kiss me.”<br>“Mean it.”<br>“I can’t.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Needless to say, the friends-with-benefits situation doesn't work for long. Jealousy, feelings and truths get in the way, but they make for a hell of a great story. With a few pre-Bianca James Cavendish cameos and kick ass side characters, this book still holds it place as one of my favorites! <br><br>TRISTAN TRISTAN TRISTAN!<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “I want you to let go. i want you to submit. I want to make you lose your mind. I want you to be so far gone that the only word left in your vocabulary is my name.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425756ra/849970.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you're looking for a fun, steamy and sexy read that still has some substance to it, drop everything and pick this up –you will not be disappointing!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394303557i/8833543._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/681425839?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Book 2 review</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743538479?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Book 3 review</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4027640956338328439" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

  <span id="freeText11942296222378436328" style="display:none">*****FIVE I LOVE TRISTAN &amp; DANIKA STARS!!!*****<br><br>Simply AMAZING!!<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/9148542_zps4c55cb53.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>I have been so intrigued by Tristan and Danika ever since they were introduced in the "Up In The Air" series.<br>I knew theirs was a story that was going to be filled with unbelievable passion and despair.<br><br>Well this book DID NOT disappoint me one bit!<br>I loved ever freaking second of reading this one.<br><br><br>This is the beginning of Tristan and Danika's crazy and passionate love affair.<br>From the very moment they meet, the chemistry is off the charts HOT!!<br><br><b>I knew that we were going to be a dangerous combination. Bad things were going to happen if we spent too much time around each other&gt;"</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/imagejpg1_zps1feeaa3c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398730124i/9456936._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zps1feeaa3c.jpg" width="350" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Danika aka "Boo", is a live in nanny/house keeper/dog walker for Bev &amp; Jerry. Two awesome people that rescued her from her god awful mother!!<br>Danika's mother is a drug addict who did very little to provide her and her sister with a good life growing up.<br>Tristan is the lead singer of a band, a club promoter, and a magician.<br>He's friends with Jerry, who has invited him to come stay at his house until his apartment is ready to be moved into.<br><br><br>Danika and Tristan become fast friends but at the same time they are majorly attracted to each other.<br>They try to keep things strictly platonic but when two people spend every waking minute together and even share a bed, things are bound to cross the line!!<br><br>HOLY SMOKES did they ever cross the line!!<br>I'm talking THREE back to back FRIGGIN chapters of SEX, SEX, oh and did I mention, SEX????? This was just one night they spend having sex!! ONE NIGHT OF SEX WAS THREE CHAPTERS LONG!!!!!!! HAHAHAHAHAHA<br>Tristan has the libido of, oh, I don't know....SUPERMAN??<br>Not that I was ever complaining!!<br>It was never too much for me! I quite enjoyed every minute of it.<br><br>That scene when Danika was using her B.O.B. on herself while Tristan was sleeping right next to her was HOT AS HELL!!!! <br><br><br>Danika and Tristan's relationship is very sexually charged, and definitely an addiction for the both of them.<br>Danika tends to have relationships with guys that are all wrong for her in hopes of finding the love she never had growing up.<br>She fights her feelings for Tristan but eventually gives in and tells him how she feels.<br><br><br><b>I was so infatuated that I feel asleep next to him, and still dreamed of him, as though being apart, even in sleep, just wasn't an option for my lovesick brain.</b><br><br><br>But Tristan doesn't believe in love.<br>He's been hurt before and he's seen what love has done to his mother.<br>This causes some tension between the two, plus the fact that Tristan has a very bad temper and extremely jealous nature when it comes to Danika. He lands in some hot water and this scares Danika.<br><br><br><br>In the end something will happen to bring the two together.<br><br><br><b>"I don't have a word for</b> <i>
  <b>this,</b>
</i> <b>because I've never felt</b> <i>
  <b>this</b>
</i> <b>before. But I do love you. I just wish there was a way to explain to you that love is just the start of it, because it's turned into so much more for me."</b><br><br><br>I know these two have a love that is bordering on obsession for one another, but I SO am rooting for these two!!!<br>I believe they are good for each other and both have been through such horrible childhoods, they deserve to find true happiness with one another.<br><br><br><br>I'm scared for what is awaiting me in book two but am so happy that all books are out so I don't have to suffer for too long!!!</span>

<div id="review_537984442" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537984442" />
    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537984442?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537984442" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8514538549245470250"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Tell me not to kiss you,” he said.<br/>“Don’t kiss me.”<br/>“Mean it.”<br/>“I can’t.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409947i/803202._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Sassy heroine, witty dialogue, dysfunctional couple… it was like my book soulmate. <br/>Tristan:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409947i/803203._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Danika:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409947i/803204._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Danika’s life has been anything but easy and now with her feet under her, she’s determined to keep it that way. <br/><i>
  <blockquote> I needed stability. I clung to it.</blockquote>
</i><br/>And then, Tristan comes barreling into her life and she learns how to let go and live in the moment. Even with the <i>Don’t List</i> they created, she falls hard and deep for</span>
  <span id="freeText8514538549245470250" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Tell me not to kiss you,” he said.<br>“Don’t kiss me.”<br>“Mean it.”<br>“I can’t.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409947i/803202._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Sassy heroine, witty dialogue, dysfunctional couple… it was like my book soulmate. <br>Tristan:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409947i/803203._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Danika:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409947i/803204._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Danika’s life has been anything but easy and now with her feet under her, she’s determined to keep it that way. <br><i>
  <blockquote> I needed stability. I clung to it.</blockquote>
</i><br>And then, Tristan comes barreling into her life and she learns how to let go and live in the moment. Even with the <i>Don’t List</i> they created, she falls hard and deep for him. <br><i>
  <blockquote>Of course, that only made her impact with the ground that much more devastating.</blockquote>
</i><br>Danika was great and very realistic character. I love how sassy she was and her no bullsh*t personality was <b>refreshing.</b> She was strong when she needed to be but also very vulnerable. <br><i>
  <blockquote> “I've been cut<br>I've been opened up<br>I've been shattered by the ones I thought I loved.”<br>-Chalk Outline, Three Days Grace<br><br>Who was I? Who was somebody like me even supposed to be? Nobody loved me. It didn’t feel like anyone ever had. So where did that leave me?</blockquote>
</i><br>Tristan was broody and mean, but his soft moments melted my heart. You could see the differences between how he was with Danika and how he was with someone else. He’s definitely a favorite of mine but I’m not seeing good things in the future for him…<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409947ra/803205.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Bad Things</i> is told from Danika’s POV and Tristan’s. I <b>felt</b> everything in this book. Every <b>happy, sad, frustrating, angry</b> moment, I felt right along with them. The dual POV just made it stronger because, even though seeing everything through Danika’s eyes affected me, Tristan was like a freight train of emotions. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “I need you. I’ve never needed anyone or anything the way I need you. I need you in a way that would break me if I lost you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><b>Their relationship was… a beautiful train wreck.</b> They’re not good for each other but there’s no doubt in my mind that they’re meant to be together. When it’s good, it’s great but when it’s bad, it’s horrendous. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409947ra/803206.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yet, I still can’t help but root for them. <br><i>
  <blockquote> “When it’s right, like it is with us, it doesn’t make your life harder, it makes it better, even when it’s hard. I’ve never been so happy as I’ve been with you, and I don’t begin to know how to get past that.”</blockquote>
</i><br>I read the <i>Up In The Air</i> series before <i>Bad Things</i> so I know where Danika and Tristan are headed. I just want to know… <b>HOW THE HELL DO THEY END UP THERE?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409947ra/803207.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> They’re obsessed with each other, their neediness practically bordering on crazy. <br>Tristan must have done something beyond stupid and I’m <b>dying</b> to know what it was. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “… you were my strength , when I was too weak to even stand.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer666911369" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11158165168731887185">I really enjoyed this story. Tristan and Danika had amazing chemistry. If you're wondering if you want to read this book, do it! It is a great read.<br/><br/>The only thing that kind of bugged me was that when they had disputes, such as Tristan's flirtatious chat with Natalie on the patio, Danika just seemed to get over it with only a few words from Tristan. Maybe I'm in the minority, but I enjoy some serious angst in a book and there's no way some of his actions would have been forgiven so easily.<br/><br/>That be</span>
  <span id="freeText11158165168731887185" style="display:none">I really enjoyed this story. Tristan and Danika had amazing chemistry. If you're wondering if you want to read this book, do it! It is a great read.<br /><br />The only thing that kind of bugged me was that when they had disputes, such as Tristan's flirtatious chat with Natalie on the patio, Danika just seemed to get over it with only a few words from Tristan. Maybe I'm in the minority, but I enjoy some serious angst in a book and there's no way some of his actions would have been forgiven so easily.<br /><br />That being said, I really enjoyed the progression of the relationship between Tristan and Danika. The characters were well-developed and the story didn't seem rushed. Danika was a strong and spirited female lead, which is a nice change from many of the weak-minded heroines that seem to be popular. When they finally got together it was hot, hot hot!<br /><br />The ending really threw me for a loop. I can't wait to read the next book in the series and see where the story goes. No doubt, the events at the end of book one will have a large influence on Tristan in the following books.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2681441234" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer77402518395686731"><b>1 star</b><br/><br/>Uhh... Wtf was this bs? <br/>The beginning to middle was a solid 4-5 stars for me cuz the MCs were likeable and the chemistry was amazing but then everything just went downhill after their <b>separation </b>.<br/><br/>First of all, <b>Danika</b> (h), is the worst nanny ever. How are her employers so sweet to her and haven’t fired her lazy ass yet? She parties and gets drunk EVERY damn night, hungover every day, goes home at 4 am then wakes up at 7 am to take care of the kids... She’s basically leeching off the ppl who</span>
  <span id="freeText77402518395686731" style="display:none"><b>1 star</b><br /><br />Uhh... Wtf was this bs? <br />The beginning to middle was a solid 4-5 stars for me cuz the MCs were likeable and the chemistry was amazing but then everything just went downhill after their <b>separation </b>.<br /><br />First of all, <b>Danika</b> (h), is the worst nanny ever. How are her employers so sweet to her and haven’t fired her lazy ass yet? She parties and gets drunk EVERY damn night, hungover every day, goes home at 4 am then wakes up at 7 am to take care of the kids... She’s basically leeching off the ppl who care for her and like, How is she surviving?<br />This is the most unrealistic shit ever. <br />How is this not talked about more in this book?<br />How can she party every night? I’m honestly surprised she didn’t get alcohol poisoning or liver failure.<br /><br />Second, I’ve never been this mad at an h since Violet from <b>At Peace</b>. Danika is supposed to be this sarcastic, independent, sassy woman, and she was... in the beginning. After that, she was just the biggest <b>pushover/doormat </b>h I’ve EVER read in a looong time. One thing I really hate is when h says they’re strong but her actions show she’s just a horny idiot. I swear, every time H hurts her and makes a mistake, he gives a half-ass apology, she EASILY forgives him, and worse, she says I LOVE YOU when the H NEVER says it back and they have make up sex All. The. Damn. Time.<br /><br />I truly feel embarrassed for her and I’m so ashamed that she’s part of the sisterhood. <br /><br />How can she forgive <b>Tristan</b> (H) who <b>slept with OW the SAME night she poured her heart out?</b><br />How can she forgive him SO EASILY for ignoring her ass for two weeks after her declaration of love, sleeping with so many women, getting drunk every night?<br />How can she be in love with a <b>hypocritical jealous asshole</b> who beats up any man who touches her and genuinely scares her? <br />How can she forgive him for outright flirting with his ex and making the “oh but it was harmless flirting” excuse?<br />How can she forgive this asshole who fucked OW just hours before they reconciled, knowing she was gonna show up at the club? <br /><br />Did we get a good grovel from all this? <b>HELL NO.</b> All he did was distract her with sex and then give a half-ass apology. What’s worse is that she gives in to the sex so easily! Wtf is this bs?! Even if there was grovelling, I would NEVER forgive this disgusting asshole. The fact that he slept with OW during their separation right after h told him she loved him AND right after they have been intimate with one another for over a week was the <b>most disgusting and unforgivable thing EVER!</b> And the fact that the OW situation is brushed off so easily?? Wtf. Why? So, he slept with so many women right after she knows he knows she loves him and she’s just gonna forgive and forget AND have sex with him so easily? Wtf is this bullshit??<br /><br />She <b>never made him work for it</b>. Literally, after weeks of not seeing him, first thing he did was make a move on her. He did NOT apologize and grovel, oh no, he thought with his dick (unsurprisingly) and the h was just a willing participant, clearly not thinking that she deserves better cuz she’s thinking with her nether region. <br /><br />I really hate heroines who are so blinded with lust (and yes, its lust, NOT love) they become the <b>biggest idiot doormat in the history of doormat heroines.</b><br /><br />And ugh. The love that they supposedly feel for one another? Yeah... that’s like the biggest lie out there.<br />All I’ve ever read is them lusting for one another and thinking about having sex all the time. <br />How in the world is this “love”? <br /><br />I have never read one intimate scene not revolving around sex in this book that made me believe the H loves h. You know why? Cuz the fact that he easily brushed off h’s love and slept with so much OW during their separation just proves he doesn’t care about her, and that honestly made him so <b>irredeemable </b> in my eyes. I never believed that he loved her. Man ho-ing his way when he knew he broke the h’s heart was the most selfish thing I’ve ever read. <br />And also, how can I believe he loved her when <b>all he wanted from her was sex</b>? I don’t see him being interested in her as a person. Every chance he gets, he tells h how sexy she is and how much he wants to fuck her and nothing else. How can I believe he genuinely has TRUE feelings for her??<br /><br />Aren’t heroes supposed to be swoony and romantic? Tristan is the biggest <b>fuckboy</b> H I’ve ever read. How can I fall in love with him when all he’s done is think with his dick? <br /><br />And let’s not even start with the h <b>fighting the OW instead of the H</b>. Uh bishh they’re not the ones who broke your heart so why tf is she fighting the OW instead of the her “boyfriend” who couldn’t keep his dick in his pants?<br /><br />And the sex scenes were hot in the beginning but they honestly just felt like <b>fillers</b>. They were not full of emotions. They were just straight out lust. <br /><br /><br />The last half of this book is the most infuriating thing I’ve ever read. I never wanted to smack someone more than I wanted to smack both Danika and Tristan.<br /><b>They’re the stupidest, horniest, dumbest MCs I have EVER read.</b><br />And wtf was that ending?</span>
  <a data-text-id="77402518395686731" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4536260090368677507">Oh boy,<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394674337ra/8887568.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>The first half of the book had me <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394674337ra/8887569.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Danika and Tristan were so funny together. There was so much lighthearted banter and teasing, it was just fun watching how they were getting to know each other. There was a lot of sexual undertones but they were determined to be friends as they just genuinely liked each other so much.<br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Didn't you know I was out here, just waiting for a friend like you?"<br/>"Of course I didn't know. I'd have been dancing on top of every bar in town, instead of studying, if I</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText4536260090368677507" style="display:none">Oh boy,<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394674337ra/8887568.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The first half of the book had me <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394674337ra/8887569.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Danika and Tristan were so funny together. There was so much lighthearted banter and teasing, it was just fun watching how they were getting to know each other. There was a lot of sexual undertones but they were determined to be friends as they just genuinely liked each other so much.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>“Didn't you know I was out here, just waiting for a friend like you?"<br>"Of course I didn't know. I'd have been dancing on top of every bar in town, instead of studying, if I'd known that."<br>"Tell me not to kiss you," he said, when his lips were a breath away from mine.<br>"Don't kiss me," I told him, my voice a breathless rasp.<br>"Mean it," he said, crowding me into the corner of the pool.<br>He tilted my chin up with his finger.<br>"I can't," I gasped.<br>The words had barely left my lips before he was kissing me.” </i>
</b><br><br><br>Oh Tristan, you beautiful man-whore you!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392389910ra/8550148.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>“I want to be with you. I’ve made it way more fucking complicated than it needs to be, and I want to un-complicate it. I’ve no right to ask it, but will you give me the chance to prove that I can be better than I’ve been?” </i>
</b><br><br><br>These two definitely have a lot of growing up to do and I have a feeling book 2 is going to destroy me. Tristan is a loose cannon right now. We will see how long they can keep it together before the shit begins to fly.....<br><br><i>BR with my wonderfully awesome pervy girls, Lanazon, Alex and Mirjana</i></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RN35qgnPtc0LEwfB13tlptuGS8XB8NlEk2mkT0kuRDwpiSCCcJKxSYWn76LtDZCBmR/M3UjRN7VxC96GO9XX8A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LaWIwd0SYgKvrInCVRl5aN5gTKY4CpgIV1y3eficL9dA8VHppE9mhiEYYaFvb4xPnPnLvrErdvm1Ps2wime8Gw==')})
  }

She was forced to see, in the most brutal of ways, that love does not con<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText8514895104473801133\" style=\"display:none\">Librarian\'s note: An alternate cover edition can be found here\n\n\nBOOK THREE: TRISTAN &amp; DANIKA THE IMPACT Tristan hit rock bottom, and no one felt the impact harder than Danika. She was forced to see, in the most brutal of ways, that love does not conquer all. Bruised, bloody, and broken she had to walk away. THE AFTERMATH Picking up the pieces of your life after a tragedy is a daunting prospect, and that’s considering you still own all of the pieces. But what if you don’t? What if someone else owns those pieces, and those pieces are a part of your soul? You dig deep and work with what you’ve got. That’s what Danika told herself and believed, every single day, for years. Tristan and Danika’s love had failed every test that life had thrown at them. She couldn’t forget that, not for one second. And if those tests had been overly harsh, well, she wasn’t one to wallow in self-pity. The failure was the thing she had to focus on. The failure was the lesson. She had no intention of working so hard to make it out of hell without learning that lesson well. THE REUNION Over six years after the night that changed everything, Danika finds herself forced to spend the weekend constantly in Tristan’s company, as they attend the wedding of two of their dearest friends. It’s been long enough that she feels they can be friendly again without it destroying her peace of mind, but just a small amount of time in his presence has her remembering something she had forced herself to forget: There’d been a reason she’d gone through hell with this man, for this man, some true good to precede the bad. She shocks herself by quickly giving in to a hunger that she never imagined could still consume her. Even the best intentioned denial has a breaking point. THE HARSH REALITY After everything that’s happened, the rise and the fall, the pain and the aftermath, can these two navigate the waters of acute regret, survive the trials of coming face to face with all that they have lost, and find the strength to try again? This book is intended for readers 18 and up.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"8514895104473801133\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n    <\/div>\n\n      <div
